[30;1m102 | [0m[35mrequest. Since only one handler will receive the request, the others will have[0m
[30;1m103 | [0m[35mbeen awakened for no reason, wasting CPU cycles. At this time, Gunicorn does[0m
[30;1m104 | [0m[35mnot implement any IPC solution for coordinating between worker processes. You[0m
